         <div class="title" model="subject" template="title">
          <h2 if="title">
           <h1>
            Suburban Chevrolet - Eden Prairie’s Preferred Chevrolet Dealership
           </h1>
          </h2>
         </div>
         <div class="copy" model="subject" template="copy">
          At Suburban Chevrolet, we put a special focus on listening to our customers’ needs. When you walk in the door, it’s our goal to make the shopping experience as easy as possible. Whether you’re looking for a car, truck or SUV, we’re confident you’ll find the right vehicle in our large inventory of Chevrolet cars. So if you’re looking for a new, used or certified pre-owned vehicle, or are interested in car service and repair, or auto financing, we’re ready to assist you. Stop in today or give us a call at (877) 350-6609.
         </div>
